      <script type="text/javascript">
       function getStatsForThemeMiniStats() {
		// Call ajax request only if data is not here.
		if ($("#upv_2644058").text() == "Loading..." ) {
			jQuery.getJSON("/stats/theme/2644058?view=json", function(json){
				jQuery("#upv_2644058").empty();
				if (json.stats &amp;&amp; json.stats.uniqueVisitors &gt;= 0) {
					jQuery("#upv_2644058").append(json.stats.uniqueVisitors);				
				} else {
					jQuery("#upv_2644058").append("Not available");
				}
			});
		}
	}

           <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
            <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="https://ekjeacheblog.com/find-dresses-cleavage-fit-depending-silhouette/" onclick="trackPostClick(4041973049 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
             Find out what dresses with cleavage fit you depending on your silhouette
            </a>
           </h2>
          </div>
          <div class="post-content clearfix ">
           <div class="post-image">
            <a href="https://ekjeacheblog.com/find-dresses-cleavage-fit-depending-silhouette/" onclick="trackPostClick(4041973049); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
             <div class="thisistherealimage">
              <img alt="Find out what dresses with cleavage fit you depending on your silhouette | Jewelry | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="320" id="postImage_4041973049" src="http://img.scoop.it/8hpznXlKabSZrcXcA_UPYzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 320;" width="224"/>

             <p>
              The shape of your silhouette plays an important role when you are choosing your outfit. That is why specialist in this domain give attention to all details. Furthermore, celebrities that have access to this type of information look amazing at special events. You can also learn to put your best features into use and hide the parts of your body that you are not really proud of.
             </p>

       jQuery(document).ready(function() {
  			var siteGuid = 'f3ee344206df0c6d0ae2ac138cf16fc8';
  			var userId = $.cookie("grvinsights");
  			if (userId == null) {
  				userId = "unknown";
  			}
  			var current_url = window.location.href;
  			var limit = 3;
  			var url = 'http://rma-api.gravity.com/v0/site/' + siteGuid + '/user/' + userId + '/stories?current_url=' + encodeURI(current_url) + '&amp;limit=' + parseInt(limit, 10) +"&amp;rec_type=sponsored" + '&amp;c=?';
  			$.ajax({
  			    type: 'GET',
  			    dataType: 'jsonp',
  			    url: url,
  			    success: function (data) {
  			    	if (data.status.httpCode == 200){
  			    		var payload = data.payload;
					var ads = jQuery(".gravity");
					jQuery(payload).each(function (index, article) {
						var adpost = jQuery(jQuery(ads).get(index));
						if (typeof(adpost) != "undefined") {
							// title
							jQuery("h2 a", adpost).attr("href", article.url).text(article.title);
							// image
							var image = jQuery(".post-image", adpost);
							jQuery("a", image).attr("href", article.url);
							jQuery("img", image).data("original", article.image).lazyload({
						    	failure_limit: 20
						    });
							// description
							jQuery(".post-description blockquote", adpost).text(article.summary);
							// domain
							
							var url = document.createElement('a');
							url.href = article.targetUrl;
							jQuery(".post-metas a", adpost).text(url.hostname).attr("href", article.url);
							// show
							adpost.show();
							
							// Is there a post to print?
							var gravityItems = jQuery("#gravity-items");
							if (gravityItems.length &gt; 0) {
								var gravityItem = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-item' /&gt;");
								
								// Image
								var gravityImage = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-image' /&gt;");
								gravityImage.css({
									backgroundImage: "url('"+article.image+"')"
								});
								gravityItem.append(gravityImage);
								gravityImage.wrap("&lt;a href='"+ article.url+"'  target='_blank' rel='nofollow' /&gt;");
								
								// Title
								var gravityTitle = jQuery("&lt;h3 &gt;"+article.title+"&lt;/h3&gt;");
								gravityItem.append(gravityTitle);
								gravityTitle.wrapInner("&lt;a href='"+ article.url+"' target='_blank' rel='nofollow'/&gt;");
								
								// Source
								var gravitySource = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-source'&gt;From &lt;/div&gt;");
								var gravitySourceA = jQuery("&lt;a /&gt;");
								gravitySourceA.attr("href", article.url);
								gravitySourceA.text(url.hostname);
								gravitySourceA.attr("target", "_blank");
								gravitySourceA.attr("rel", "nofollow");
								
								gravitySource.append(gravitySourceA);
								gravityItem.append(gravitySource);
								
								// Track click
								jQuery("a", gravityItem).each(function() {
									jQuery(this).click(function() {
										trackClick("clickOnGravityAds", function() {return true;}, null);
									});
								});
								
								gravityItems.append(gravityItem);
							}
						}
					});
					jQuery("#gravity-items").fadeIn();
  			    	} else {
  			    	}
  			       
  			    },
  			    error: function (e) {
  			    }
  			});
  		});
      </script>
     </div>
    </div>

function googlePlusTouched(e) {
	if (e.state == "on") {
		var url = e.href;
		var location = "bottomOfPost";
		trackNativeButtonShare('google', location, url);
	}

function loadSocialWidgetInAPost(post) {
	if (post.length &gt; 0) {
		//facebook
		if (typeof FB != 'undefined') {
			FB.XFBML.parse(jQuery(".share-button-fb",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-fb");
		}
		//twitter
		if (typeof twttr != 'undefined') {
			jQuery(".share-button-tw a", post).addClass("twitter-share-button");
			twttr.widgets.load(jQuery(".share-button-tw",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-tw");
		}
		//G+
		if (typeof gapi != 'undefined') {
			gapi.plusone.go(jQuery(".share-button-gp",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-gp");
		}
	}
}


function loadVisibleSharers() {
	jQuery(".post").each(function(){
		var elt = jQuery(this);
		if (elt.attr("id") == "topic-tags-widget") {
			return;
		}
		if (elt.hasClass("loaded-tw") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-gp") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-fb")) {return;}
		if (elt.isOnScreen()) {
			loadSocialWidgetInAPost(elt);
		}
	});
}

jQuery(window).bind("resize", function(event) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

var scrollingChecker = 0;
function onScroll(event) {
	clearTimeout(scrollingChecker);
	scrollingChecker = setTimeout(onStopScrolling, 300);
}

function onStopScrolling() {
	loadVisibleSharers();
}

jQuery(document).bind("scroll", onScroll);

     e.parentNode.insertBefore(n, e);
   })(document,"script","hs-analytics",300000);
